right to counsel and the administration of indigent defense services in Washington. I. R IGHT TO COUNSEL The Sixth Amendment to the United States Constitution states that “[i]n all criminal prosecutions, the accused shall enjoy the right to . . . have the assistance of counsel for his defens e.” The right to counsel is a fundamental right, and thus , it imposes an obligatory duty on to the states to provide counsel to indigent defendants through the Fourteenth Amendment. Gideon v. Wainwright , 372 U.S. 335, 342- 44,
